Code:
#include<libintl.h>
        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !0 && !defined(dcgettext) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_dcgettext found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_dcgettext)
                #error "__builtin_dcgettext not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(dcgettext)
            __builtin_dcgettext;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }

        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !1 && !defined(glTexDirectVIV) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_glTexDirectVIV found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_glTexDirectVIV)
                #error "__builtin_glTexDirectVIV not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(glTexDirectVIV)
            __builtin_glTexDirectVIV;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }

Code:
 #include<libintl.h>
        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !0 && !defined(dcgettext) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_dcgettext found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_dcgettext)
                #error "__builtin_dcgettext not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(dcgettext)
            __builtin_dcgettext;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }
